jQuery(document).ready(function($){

var initList = setInterval(function animation(){
	$('#custCareTpSlider .sldToTop4').each(function(){
		$(this).animate({

				clone=$(this).clone();

			})

         <script type="text/javascript">
          var $=jQuery.noConflict();
function changeCurrency(currencyObj,catId)
{	
	$('.loading_image_div').css('top',$(window).scrollTop()+250);
	$('#loading').height($(document).height());
	$('#loading').show();
	$('.loadingText').show();
	$(".currencydropdown dd ul.currencySelect").hide();
	var param ="";
	var currUrl = $('#currencyURL').val();
	param = $('#currencyParams').val();
	var selectedCurrency = currencyObj.innerText;
	if(selectedCurrency == null || selectedCurrency == 'undefined')
		selectedCurrency = currencyObj.textContent;
	
	if(selectedCurrency !=null){
		var length = selectedCurrency.length;
		var currency = selectedCurrency.substring(length-3,length);
		if(param == 'null'){
			var url = currUrl + "?catalogueID="+catId+"&amp;selCur="+currency;
		}
		else{
			var url = currUrl + "?"+param+"&amp;selCur="+currency;
		}
		window.location.href = url;
	}
}
function currencyLink(){
	$(".currencydropdown dd ul.currencySelect").toggle();
}
function currencyLink1(){
	$("#currencydropdown1 dd ul#currencySelect1").toggle();
}
         </script>

      <script type="text/javascript">
       function highlightTop(id){
	var result = null;
	var finalId=id;
	if(id.indexOf('Book') !== -1 ){
		result = id.replace("cshowBook", "subMenu_Book"); 
		finalId=id.replace("subMenu_", "cshow"); 
	}
	else{
		result = id.replace("cshow", "subMenu_"); 
		finalId=id.replace("subMenu_", "cshow"); 

	}
	if ($("#"+result).css('display') == 'none') {
		$("#"+finalId).removeClass( "activeLeft" );
		$("#"+finalId).addClass( "normalLeft" );
	}
	else{
		$("#"+finalId).addClass( "activeLeft" );
	}
}
      </script>

      <div id="prodListLeftPanel">
       <script type="text/javascript">
        var jqSlider=jQuery.noConflict();  
  jqSlider(document).ready(function() {
	  var callSearch = true;
	  var startPrice = jqSlider("#startPrice").val();
	  var min1 = Number(startPrice);
	  var endPrice = jqSlider("#endPrice").val();
	  var max1 = Number(endPrice);
	  
	  if( typeof startPrice != 'undefined'){
		  if(startPrice.indexOf(".") != -1 &amp;&amp; startPrice.substr(startPrice.length - 1)=="0")
			  min1 = Number(min1 + 0.001);
      }

	  if( typeof endPrice != 'undefined'){
		  if(endPrice.indexOf(".") != -1 &amp;&amp; endPrice.substr(endPrice.length - 1)=="0")
			   max1 = Number(endPrice.replace(endPrice.substr(endPrice.length - 2),Number(endPrice.substr(endPrice.length - 2))-1));
	  }
	  

	  if(min1 == max1){
	     max1 =  min1 + 1;
	     jqSlider("#endPrice").val(max1);	
	  }
	  
	  jqSlider("#slider").slider({
      range: true,
      min: min1,
      max: max1,
      values: [min1, max1],
      slide: function(event, ui) {
    	  $("#startPrice").val(ui.values[0]);	
    	  $("#endPrice").val(ui.values[1]);	
      },
      change:function(event, ui){
    	  jqSlider("#selprice").html("");
    	  //$("#selprice").append("&lt;ul id='selPrc' class='chosenPrc'&gt;&lt;li class='special'&gt;&lt;span class='colorBox' style='width:auto;'&gt;"+$('#slider').slider('values', 0)+ " - "+$('#slider').slider('values', 1)+"&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class='remove-icon' id='priceCls'&gt;X&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;");
    	  if(callSearch){
    		  jqSlider("#applyPriceFilter").html("Y");
    		  narrowSearch('searchResultDisplay');  
    	  }
    	  jqSlider("#clearAllDiv").show();
      	}
		});
	  /*$("#startPrice").val($("#slider").slider("values", 0));
	  $("#endPrice").val($("#slider").slider("values", 1));*/
	  
	  jqSlider("#priceCls").live('click',function(){		 
		  jqSlider("#startPrice").val(min1);
		  jqSlider("#endPrice").val(max1);	
		  callSearch = false;
		  jqSlider("#slider").slider("values", 0, min1);
		  callSearch = true;
		  jqSlider("#slider").slider("values", 1, max1);
    	  jqSlider("#selprice").html("");
	  });
	  jqSlider("#clearAllDiv").live('click',function(){		 
		  jqSlider("#startPrice").val(min1);
		  jqSlider("#endPrice").val(max1);	
		  callSearch = false;
		  jqSlider("#slider").slider("values", 0, min1);		  
		  jqSlider("#slider").slider("values", 1, max1);    	  
    	  jqSlider("#selprice").html("");
		  callSearch = true;
	  }); 
	  
  });
       </script>

       <script type="text/javascript">
        function hideOthers(spanId,obj){
	var tempSpan = document.getElementById("openSpan").value;
	var temp = document.getElementById('openTab').value;
	if(tempSpan !=''){
		if(document.getElementById("openSpan").className == 'clm2Act'){
			document.getElementById("openSpan").className = 'clm2Nor';
		}
	}
	if(temp !='' &amp;&amp; temp != obj){
		if(document.getElementById('openTab').style.display == 'block'){
			document.getElementById('openTab').style.display = 'none';
		}
		
	}
	document.getElementById('openTab').value=obj;
	document.getElementById("openSpan").value = spanId.id;
}

function treeHideShow1(object,divId){
	if(object != null){
		var displayStatus;
		var id;
		var subLevelCategories = new Array();
		var list = document.getElementsByTagName('div');
		var spanList = document.getElementsByTagName('span');
		var filterSpanList = new Array();
		var value = -1;
		for(var counter = 0; counter &lt; spanList.length; counter++){
			if(spanList[counter].id.indexOf('_tree') != -1){
				filterSpanList[++value] = spanList[counter];
			}
		}
		var divId = document.getElementById(divId);
		if(divId.style.display == 'none'){
			divId.style.display = 'block';
			//object.innerHTML = '-';
			(divId+'_Category').className = 'clm2Act';
		}else{
			divId.style.display = 'none';
			//object.innerHTML = '+';
			$(divId+'_Category').className = 'clm2Nor';
		}
		/** Need to uncomment the below code in case dont want to use + sign &amp; need to comment above code	**/
		/*if(
(divId).style.display == 'block'){
			$(divId).style.display = 'none';
		}else{
			$(divId).style.display = 'block';
		}*/


		id = object.id;
		if(id.indexOf('level_2') != -1 &amp;&amp; id.indexOf('_tree') != -1){
			for(var count = 0; count &lt; list.length; count++){
				if(list[count].id.indexOf('level_2') != -1){
					for(var counter = 0; counter &lt; filterSpanList.length; counter++){
						if(filterSpanList[counter].id.indexOf(list[count].id) != -1){
							if(list[count].id.indexOf(id.substring(0,id.indexOf('_tree'))) != -1){		
							}else{
								filterSpanList[counter].innerHTML = "-";
								//list[count].style.display = 'block';
								treeDivHideShow1(filterSpanList[counter],list[count].id);		
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}			
	}
}
       </script>

        <script type="text/javascript">
         function addProductId(productID)
{
	if(productIds == null)
		productIds = productID+"-";
	else
		productIds = productIds+productID+"-";
}
function submitForm()
{
	var c=0;
	var cbox = document.getElementsByTagName('input');
	for (var i = 0; i &lt; cbox.length; i++){
		if(cbox[i].type=="checkbox"){
			if(cbox[i].checked)
              c =c+1;
		}
	}
	if(c==1 || c==0){
		alert("Select at least two products to compare");
		return false;
	}else if(c&gt;3){
		alert("Maximum 3 products can be comapred at a time");
		return false;
	}else{
	document.getElementById("cProducts").value=productIds;
	document.getElementById("form1").submit();
	}
}
        </script>

         var $=jQuery.noConflict();
var count=1;
var clone;
var parent,feedbackLength;
jQuery(document).ready(function($){
var initList = setInterval(function(){
	 $('#custCareTpSlider2 .sldToTop2').each(function(){
		$(this).animate({
			'top':'-=125px'}
			,500,
			function(){
			var top=parseInt($(this).css('top').replace('px',''))+parseInt($(this).css('width').replace('px',''));
			
			
				 clone=$(this).clone();
				
				 parent=$(this).parent(); 
                			
				 clone.slideUp(); 
				 $(this).remove();
				 parent.append(clone);  
		
			
			
			feedbackLength = $("#feedbackLength").val();
			
			 if(count==feedbackLength){
				 count=1;
				 clone.css('top','0px');
				
			 }
			 count=count+1;
			})
			})
			},6000); 
			
 
$('#custCareTpSlider2').mouseover(function(){
    clearInterval(initList);
 }).mouseout(function(){
	 var count1=1;
	 var clone1;
	 var parent1,feedbackLength1;
    initList = setInterval(function(){	
    	$('#custCareTpSlider2 .sldToTop2').each(function(){
    		$(this).animate({
    			'top':'-=125px'}
    			,500,
    			function(){
    			var top=parseInt($(this).css('top').replace('px',''))+parseInt($(this).css('width').replace('px',''));
    			
    			 clone1=$(this).clone();
				 parent1=$(this).parent(); 
				
				clone1.slideUp();
				$(this).remove();
				parent1.append(clone1); 
		
			    count1=count1+1;
			
			    feedbackLength1 = $("#feedbackLength").val();
			
			    if(count1==feedbackLength1){
				   count1=1;
				   clone1.css('top','0px');
			    }
    			/* if($("#custCareTpSlider2 .sldToTop2").css("top")==-250+"px")
    			{
    				var clone=$(this).clone();
    				var parent=$(this).parent();
    				clone.css('top','0px');
    				clone.slideUp();
    				$(this).remove();
    				parent.append(clone);
    			} */
    			})
    			})
    			},6000);
 })
});
